11. Models Registry
Every Eloquent model lives in its domain's Models/ folder. Models contain: relationships, casts, scopes, fillable/guarded, and trait declarations ONLY. Zero business logic inside models — all logic in Services and Actions.
RULE
Model rules: No business logic. No complex queries. No HTTP/Request references.
All money columns cast to Money value object via custom Eloquent cast.
All models with financial data have: HasLedgerEntry trait (auto-creates ledger entries on save).
All user-data models have: BelongsToTenant trait (auto-injects tenant_id scope on all queries).
Model
Domain
Key Relationships
Traits

12. Service Providers & Console Commands
12.1 Service Providers
app/Providers/
|-- AppServiceProvider.php              # Singleton bindings, macro registrations
|-- AuthServiceProvider.php            # Policy -> Model mappings
|-- EventServiceProvider.php           # Event -> Listener mappings (all 30+ events)
|-- RouteServiceProvider.php           # API route binding, rate limit definitions
|-- RepositoryServiceProvider.php      # Interface -> Implementation bindings
|-- DomainServiceProvider.php          # Domain Service singleton registrations
`-- TelescopeServiceProvider.php       # Laravel Telescope (staging only)
KEY
RepositoryServiceProvider.php is critical — it binds every Interface -> Implementation.
Example: $this->app->bind(GoalRepositoryInterface::class, EloquentGoalRepository::class)
This allows swapping Eloquent for any other ORM/storage without touching domain code.
DomainServiceProvider registers Services as singletons (stateless, safe to share across requests).
12.2 Artisan Commands

|   |-- Maintenance/
|   |   |-- ArchiveOldTransactionsCommand.php

|   |   `-- ProcessPendingDataDeletionsCommand.php
|   |-- Exchange/

`-- Kernel.php                                     # Cron schedule definitions

13. Test Structure
Tests mirror the domain structure. Architecture tests enforce DDD boundaries (PHPStan + custom rules). Unit tests cover domain services in isolation. Feature tests cover full API request-response cycle.
tests/

|   |   |-- FinancialYearTest.php           # April-March boundary tests

|   |-- Income/
|   |   `-- IncomeCalculationServiceTest.php
|   |-- Goal/
|   |   |-- GoalProjectionServiceTest.php   # TVM calculations with inflation
|   |   `-- TimeValueOfMoneyServiceTest.php
|   |-- Investment/
|   |   |-- XirrCalculationServiceTest.php  # XIRR against known SIP scenarios
|   |   `-- CagrCalculationServiceTest.php

`-- Architecture/
    |-- DomainLayerHasNoDependencyOnHttpTest.php   # Domain has no Laravel HTTP imports
    `-- ControllersAreSlimTest.php                 # Controllers max 7 lines per method
COVERAGE
Target: > 90% line coverage on Domain Services and Actions.
Every API endpoint has at least: happy path test + cross-user BOLA test + validation error test.
Architecture tests run in CI: detect if Domain layer accidentally imports app/ or Http/ classes.
LedgerIntegrityTest: after every test that creates money movement, assert ledger debits === credits.

Middleware Stack
Endpoints Covered
/api/v1/auth
Public (rate: 5/min)
register, login, forgot-password, reset-password, email/verify, email/resend
/api/v1/auth (auth)
Auth required
logout, logout-all, me, 2fa/enable, 2fa/confirm, 2fa/disable, devices
/api/v1/income
Auth + Idempotency
sources CRUD, entries CRUD, summary
/api/v1/expenses
Auth + Idempotency
CRUD, categories CRUD, budgets CRUD, summary
/api/v1/savings
Auth + Idempotency
accounts CRUD, deposit, withdraw, transactions, summary
/api/v1/emergency-fund
Auth + Idempotency
setup, update, deposit, gap-analysis
/api/v1/goals
Auth + Idempotency
CRUD, contributions CRUD, projection, reorder

Auth + Idempotency
CRUD, transactions, sip-schedules, portfolio-summary
/api/v1/debts
Auth + Idempotency
CRUD, payments, schedule, prepayment, foreclosure, payoff-strategy

Auth (rate: 3/min)

Auth + Cache
summary, net-worth-history, income-vs-expense, goal-summary, budget-alerts

Auth
profile, avatar, password, consents, data-export, deletion request/cancel
/api/v1/lookup
Auth (cached 1hr)
income-types, debt-types, goal-types, saving-types, payment-modes
/api/v1/admin
Admin + IP allowlist
users CRUD, plans CRUD, categories, investment-types, audit-logs, stats
14.2 Route File Responsibilities
File / Class
Responsibility
routes/api.php
All /api/v1/* routes. Versioned prefix. Middleware groups applied per section.
routes/auth.php
Auth-specific routes included from api.php. Keeps auth routes in one place.
routes/admin.php
Admin-only routes. Included from api.php behind RequireAdminRole + AdminIpAllowlist.
routes/web.php
Blade/web routes for login, register pages. SPA fallback route if applicable.
routes/channels.php
Broadcast channels authorization (Laravel Echo + Pusher/Soketi).
VER
API versioning: all routes prefixed with /api/v1/. When v2 launches, /api/v2/ routes in a new file.
v1 routes remain fully functional. No breaking changes to v1 when v2 is introduced.
Controller namespace: App\Http\Controllers\Api\V1\{Domain}\{Controller}

15.2 Configuration Files
File / Class
Responsibility
config/app.php
App name, timezone (Asia/Kolkata), locale (en_IN), encryption key
config/auth.php
Guards (sanctum for API), password broker, provider (users table)
config/database.php
MySQL primary + read replica connections, Redis configuration
config/cache.php
Redis as default driver. Cache key prefix per environment.
config/queue.php
Redis queue driver. 4 queues: default, reports, nightly, critical.
config/filesystems.php
S3 as default disk. Local disk for temp files. Signed URL config.
config/mail.php
SMTP/Mailgun/SES configuration. From address and name.
config/sanctum.php
Token expiry: 30 days app, 8 hours web. Stateful domains list.
config/logging.php
JSON log format. Separate channels: daily, slack, sentry.
config/horizon.php
Queue worker config: 4 queues, worker counts per queue, timeouts.
config/permission.php
Spatie permission cache duration. Table names.
config/ffp.php
Custom app config: admin_allowed_ips, dpdp_deletion_days=30, budget_warning_pct=80, sip_reminder_days=3, snapshot_retention_years=10
16. Naming Conventions
Consistent naming is a DDD requirement — it enables ubiquitous language across code, docs, and conversations. Every team member should be able to guess a class name from its description and vice versa.
Class Type
Convention + Examples
Actions
Verb + Noun + Action: CreateIncomeEntryAction, RecordDebtPaymentAction, GenerateMonthlyReportAction
Services
Noun + Service: GoalProjectionService, AmortizationService, XirrCalculationService
Repositories
Eloquent + Entity + Repository: EloquentGoalRepository, EloquentDebtPaymentRepository
Contracts
Entity + RepositoryInterface: GoalRepositoryInterface, DebtRepositoryInterface
DTOs
Entity + Data (input) or EntitySummary + Data (output): GoalData, GoalSummaryData
Events
Past tense noun phrase: GoalCompleted, BudgetExceeded, DebtPaymentRecorded
Listeners
Verb + Object + Listener: SendGoalCompletedEmailListener, WriteLedgerEntryListener
Jobs
Verb + Object + Job: ComputeXirrForInvestmentJob, GenerateMonthlyReportJob
Notifications
Noun + Notification: GoalMilestoneNotification, EmiReminderNotification
Controllers
Entity + Controller: IncomeEntryController, AmortizationScheduleController
Requests
Http verb + Entity + Request: StoreExpenseRequest, UpdateGoalRequest
Resources
Entity + Resource/Collection: InvestmentResource, InvestmentCollection
Policies
Entity + Policy: DebtPolicy, FinancialGoalPolicy
Commands
Verb + Object + Command: ComputeHealthScoresCommand, SendEmiRemindersCommand
Exceptions
Noun + Exception: GoalNotFoundException, InsufficientSavingBalanceException
Enums
Entity + StatusEnum or TypeEnum: GoalStatusEnum, AssetClassEnum
ValueObjects
Domain noun: Money, Percentage, FinancialYear, DeviceFingerprint, TenantId
Traits
Has + Feature: HasUlid, HasAuditLog, HasLedgerEntry, BelongsToTenant
RULE
No generic names: No "Manager", "Handler", "Helper", "Util" classes. Every name describes its exact responsibility.
No abbreviations: "GoalContribution" not "GoalContrib". "AmortizationSchedule" not "AmorSched".
Domain language first: use terms from the financial domain, not technical terms. "recordPayment" not "savePayment".
One class per file, one responsibility per class. File name === class name (PSR-4).

How to Read This Document
Each module in this document follows the same 8-section structure, making it easy to locate specific information quickly:
X.1 User Journey
Narrative description of the complete user experience from entry to completion
X.2 Screen Flow
Step-by-step table: Screen Name | User Action | System Response — every interaction documented
X.3 Success Scenario
The happy path — what happens when everything works correctly, step by step
X.4 Failure Scenarios
Edge cases and error states with HTTP status codes and exact error messages shown to users
X.5 Validation Rules
Every form field with its Laravel validation rule string and the user-facing error message
X.6 Notifications
Every notification trigger with channel (In-App / Email / Push) and message template
X.7 API Calls
Method, endpoint, request payload, response shape, and authentication requirement
X.8 Database Operations
Table name, SQL operation type (INSERT/UPDATE/SELECT/DELETE), and full description
Mermaid Diagrams
Every module includes a flow diagram in Mermaid syntax. To render any diagram:
Copy the diagram text starting with "flowchart TD"
Paste into https://mermaid.live or any Mermaid-compatible editor
The diagram renders as an interactive, exportable SVG flow chart
Diagrams can also be embedded in GitHub README files, Notion, and Confluence directly
API Authentication
Public
No authentication required. Open endpoint.
Auth
Requires valid Sanctum Bearer token in Authorization header
Partial-Auth
Requires partial auth state (credentials verified, 2FA pending)
Signed URL
Laravel signed URL validation (email verification links)
Admin
Requires admin role + separate admin token with IP allowlist
Response Envelope Standard
Success (single)
{ "data": { ... }, "message": "Success" }
Success (list)
{ "data": [...], "meta": { "total": n, "per_page": 15, "next_cursor": "..." } }
Validation Error
{ "message": "Validation failed", "errors": { "field": ["error message"] } }
Auth Error
{ "message": "Unauthenticated" } — HTTP 401
Forbidden
{ "message": "Forbidden" } — HTTP 403
Not Found
{ "message": "Resource not found" } — HTTP 404
Server Error
{ "message": "Something went wrong. Please try again." } — HTTP 500
REG
MODULE 1:  User Registration
1.1 User Journey
A new visitor discovers the Financial Freedom Planner, navigates to the registration page, creates an account by providing personal details, verifies their email, completes their financial profile setup, and lands on the onboarding dashboard for the first time.
1.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Landing Page
Clicks "Get Started Free"
Navigate to /register
2
Registration Form
Fills name, email, password, phone
Real-time inline validation on each field
3
Registration Form
Clicks "Create Account"
Show loading spinner, call POST /auth/register
4
Email Verification
Receives verification email, clicks link
Token validated, account activated
5
Profile Setup
Selects currency (INR default), timezone
Saves preferences, creates default expense categories
6
Onboarding Screen
Views "Setup your financial profile" wizard
Show 4-step guide: Income > Expenses > Goals > Emergency Fund
7
Dashboard
Completes or skips onboarding
Full dashboard rendered with empty state prompts
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Visitor lands on site]) --> B[Click Get Started Free]
  B --> C[/Registration Form/]
  C --> D{Validation OK?}
  D -- No --> E[Show inline errors] --> C
  D -- Yes --> F[POST /auth/register]
  F --> G{Email unique?}
  G -- No --> H[Email already exists error] --> C
  G -- Yes --> I[Create user record]
  I --> J[Send verification email]
  J --> K[/Email Sent screen/]
  K --> L{User clicks link?}
  L -- Expired --> M[Resend email] --> J
  L -- Valid --> N[Activate account]
  N --> O[/Profile Setup wizard/]
  O --> P[Save currency + timezone]
  P --> Q[/Onboarding Guide/]
  Q --> R([Dashboard - empty state])
1.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Step 1
User fills all fields correctly: name (Rahul Sharma), email (rahul@gmail.com), password (8+ chars), phone (9876543210)
Step 2
System validates all inputs pass, email is unique in users table, password meets complexity
Step 3
Account created: users table INSERT, default role assigned (user), welcome email queued
Step 4
User clicks email link within 60 minutes: email_verified_at updated, session created
Step 5
Profile setup: currency=INR, timezone=Asia/Kolkata saved, 10 default expense categories seeded
Step 6
Onboarding completed or skipped: user lands on dashboard with empty-state prompts for each module
Outcome
User fully registered, verified, and ready to add their first income source
1.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Duplicate Email
email already exists in users table -> 422 Unprocessable, highlight email field with "This email is already registered. Try logging in."
Weak Password
password fails complexity check -> 422, "Password must be at least 8 characters with one number and one letter"
Invalid Phone
phone does not match Indian mobile regex -> 422, "Enter a valid 10-digit Indian mobile number starting with 6-9"
Expired Email Link
verification token older than 60 min -> 410 Gone, show "Link expired" page with Resend button
Already Verified
user clicks link again after verifying -> redirect to login with "Account already verified"
Server Error
DB unavailable during register -> 500, generic "Something went wrong" with retry, log to Sentry
Rate Limit Hit
more than 5 registration attempts from same IP in 1 hour -> 429, "Too many attempts. Try again in 60 minutes"
1.5 Validation Rules
Field
Rule
Error Message
name
required|string|min:2|max:100|regex:/^[a-zA-Z .'-]+$/
Name must be 2-100 characters, letters only
email
required|email|max:150|unique:users,email
Enter a valid email address
password
required|string|min:8|max:128|confirmed|regex:/[0-9]/
Password must be 8+ chars with at least one number
phone
nullable|regex:/^[6-9][0-9]{9}$/
Enter a valid 10-digit Indian mobile number
currency
nullable|string|size:3|in:INR,USD,EUR,GBP,AED
Select a valid currency
timezone
nullable|timezone|max:50
Select a valid timezone
password_confirmation
required|same:password
Passwords do not match

LOG
MODULE 2:  User Login & Authentication
2.1 User Journey
A registered user navigates to the login page, enters credentials, optionally completes 2FA verification, and arrives at the dashboard. The system detects new devices, enforces rate limits, and maintains a secure session with a defined token TTL.
2.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Login Page
Enters email and password
Real-time field validation, no submission yet
2
Login Page
Clicks "Sign In"
POST /auth/login, show loading state
3
2FA Screen
If 2FA enabled: enter 6-digit TOTP code
Validate TOTP against stored secret
4
New Device Alert
If new device/IP: prompted to trust device
Send email notification of new login
5
Dashboard
Successful auth redirects to dashboard
Load user data, set session, record login event
6
Forgot Password
Clicks "Forgot Password" link
Navigate to /forgot-password
7
Reset Form
Enters email address
POST /auth/forgot-password, send reset email
8
Reset Password
Opens reset link, enters new password
POST /auth/reset-password, invalidate old tokens
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Login Page]) --> B[Enter email + password]
  B --> C[POST /auth/login]
  C --> D{Credentials valid?}
  D -- No --> E{Attempt count?}
  E -- Under 5 --> F[Show invalid credentials] --> A
  E -- 5+ --> G[Lock account 15 min] --> A
  D -- Yes --> H{2FA enabled?}
  H -- Yes --> I[/2FA Code Screen/]
  I --> J{TOTP valid?}
  J -- No --> K[Invalid code error] --> I
  J -- Yes --> L{New device?}
  H -- No --> L
  L -- Yes --> M[Log login_event + send alert email]
  L -- No --> N[Record login_event]
  M --> O[Create Sanctum token]
  N --> O
  O --> P([Dashboard])
2.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Step 1
User enters valid email and correct password on login form
Step 2
POST /auth/login returns 200 with Sanctum token (TTL: 30 days for app, 8 hours for web)
Step 3
If 2FA enabled: user enters TOTP code from authenticator app, verified against two_factor_secret
Step 4
Login event logged: login_events INSERT with IP, country_code, device_type, success=1
Step 5
Token stored in HttpOnly cookie (web) or returned in response body (API/mobile)
Step 6
Dashboard loads with user financial data from Redis cache or DB snapshot
Outcome
User authenticated, session active, last_login_at updated in users table
2.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Wrong Password
401 Unauthorized, failed_login_count incremented, "Invalid email or password"
Account Locked
423 Locked, "Account locked due to too many failed attempts. Try again after 15 minutes"
Email Not Verified
403 Forbidden, "Please verify your email before logging in" with resend link
Invalid 2FA Code
422, "Invalid code. Check your authenticator app or use a backup code"
Expired Token
401 on API call, "Session expired. Please login again" -> redirect to login
Account Suspended
403, "Your account has been suspended. Contact support@ffplanner.in"
Rate Limit
429, "Too many login attempts. Try again in 15 minutes"
2.5 Validation Rules
Field
Rule
Error Message
email
required|email|max:150
Enter a valid email address
password
required|string|min:8|max:128
Password is required
otp_code
required_if:2fa_enabled,true|string|size:6|numeric
Enter the 6-digit code from your authenticator
device_name
nullable|string|max:100
Device name must be under 100 characters

2.8 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
SELECT
users
WHERE email=? AND deleted_at IS NULL, check password hash
UPDATE
users
SET failed_login_count=0, last_login_at=NOW() on success
UPDATE
users
SET failed_login_count=failed_login_count+1 on failure
UPDATE
users
SET account_locked_until=NOW()+15min after 5 failures
INSERT
login_events
ip, country_code, device_type, browser, success, failure_reason
INSERT
trusted_devices
On new device confirmation: fingerprint, device_name, trusted_at
UPDATE
users
SET password=bcrypt(new), last_login_at on password reset
DELETE
personal_access_tokens
WHERE tokenable_id=user_id on logout-all
DSH
MODULE 3:  Dashboard
3.1 User Journey
After login the user lands on their personal financial command centre. The dashboard aggregates data from all modules into a single real-time view: net worth, income vs expenses, savings progress, investment performance, goal completion, and debt status — all with contextual insights and quick-action shortcuts.
3.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Dashboard Home
Page loads after login
Fetch summary from Redis cache (TTL 15 min) or snapshot
2
KPI Cards Row
Views 6 metric cards at top
Display: Net Worth, Monthly Income, Monthly Expense, Savings Rate, Investment Value, Total Debt
3
Net Worth Chart
Views historical net worth trend graph
Load from financial_snapshots, last 12 months
4
Income vs Expense
Views bar chart current month
Aggregate income_entries and expenses for current month
5
Goals Widget
Sees all active goals with progress bars
Load top 4 goals by priority with completion %
6
Quick Actions
Clicks "Add Expense", "Log Income", etc.
Open modal or navigate to respective module
7
Notifications Bell
Sees unread count badge, clicks to expand
Load last 5 unread notifications from DB
8
Alerts Banner
Budget exceeded alert shown inline
Show warning if any category >80% budget used
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([User logs in]) --> B[GET /dashboard/summary]
  B --> C{Cache hit?}
  C -- Yes --> D[Return Redis cached data]
  C -- No --> E[Query financial_snapshots]
  E --> F[Compute current-month delta]
  F --> G[Cache result 15 min]
  G --> D
  D --> H[/Dashboard rendered/]
  H --> I[Load KPI cards]
  H --> J[Load charts async]
  H --> K[Check budget alerts]
  K --> L{Any category over 80%?}
  L -- Yes --> M[Show budget warning banner]
  L -- No --> N[No alert]
  H --> O[Load top goals]
  H --> P[Load notification count]
3.3 Dashboard KPI Definitions
Net Worth
SUM(savings + investments) - SUM(active debts outstanding_amount)
Monthly Income
SUM(income_entries.amount) WHERE month=current, year=current
Monthly Expenses
SUM(expenses.amount) WHERE month=current, year=current
Savings Rate %
((Monthly Income - Monthly Expenses) / Monthly Income) * 100
Investment Value
SUM(investments.current_value) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL
Total Debt
SUM(debts.outstanding_amount) WHERE status=active
Emergency Fund %
(emergency_funds.current_amount / required_amount) * 100
Goal Progress
AVG(current_amount/target_amount * 100) across active goals
3.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Cache Hit
Dashboard loads in <200ms from Redis cache. All 6 KPIs displayed correctly
Cache Miss
Dashboard loads in <800ms from financial_snapshots + current-month delta queries
Charts Loaded
Async chart data loads within 1 second. Net worth trend shows 12-month line graph
Alerts Working
Food budget at 85% -> yellow warning banner "You have used 85% of your Food budget"
Goals Visible
Top 4 goals shown with progress bars, next milestone highlighted
Outcome
User has full financial visibility on one screen with no manual calculations needed
3.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Cache Down
Redis unavailable -> fallback to DB query, dashboard loads in ~1.5s, no error shown to user
No Data Yet
New user with no transactions -> empty state with contextual "Add your first salary" prompts
Stale Cache
Cache not invalidated after large data import -> show "Refresh" button with last_updated timestamp
Chart API Fails
Chart endpoint 500 -> charts show skeleton with "Could not load chart. Tap to retry"
Slow DB
DB query >3s -> show partial data with loading spinners for pending sections
3.5 Notifications / Alerts shown on Dashboard
Trigger
Channel
Message
Budget over 80%
Banner
You have used {pct}% of your {category} budget this month.
Budget over 100%
Banner
You exceeded your {category} budget by Rs.{amount}.
Goal behind schedule
Banner
Your "{goal}" goal is Rs.{amount} behind this month target.
Emergency fund low
Banner
Your emergency fund covers only {n} months. Recommended: 6 months.
EMI due in 3 days
Banner
Your {loan} EMI of Rs.{amount} is due on {date}.
No income this month
Banner
No income recorded this month. Add your salary entry.

3.7 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
SELECT
financial_snapshots
WHERE user_id=? ORDER BY snapshot_date DESC LIMIT 12
SELECT
income_entries
SUM(amount) WHERE user_id=? AND month=? AND year=?
SELECT
expenses
SUM(amount) WHERE user_id=? AND month=? AND year=?
SELECT
investments
SUM(current_value) WHERE user_id=? AND deleted_at IS NULL
SELECT
debts
SUM(outstanding_amount) WHERE user_id=? AND status=active
SELECT
financial_goals
WHERE user_id=? AND status=active ORDER BY priority LIMIT 4
SELECT
expense_budgets
JOIN expenses for budget utilization calculation
SET
Redis cache
dashboard:user:{id}:summary = JSON payload, EX 900 (15 min TTL)
SAL
MODULE 4:  Salary & Income Management
4.1 User Journey
The user creates one or more income sources (salary job, freelance project, rental property), then records actual income entries against each source. The system calculates monthly and yearly income totals, tracks income trends, and feeds data to the dashboard and reports.
4.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Income Home
Clicks "Income" in sidebar
Load income sources list + current month total
2
Add Source
Clicks "+ Add Income Source"
Open modal: title, type, recurring toggle, default amount
3
Source Created
Submits source form
POST /income/sources, show source in list
4
Record Income
Clicks "Record Income" on a source
Open entry modal: amount, date, notes, attachment
5
Entry Saved
Submits income entry
POST /income/entries, update monthly total
6
Income History
Scrolls income entries list
Paginated list, filterable by month/year/source
7
Edit Entry
Clicks edit icon on an entry
Load entry into modal, PUT /income/entries/{id}
8
Monthly Summary
Clicks "Summary" tab
Show income by source type breakdown, YoY comparison
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Income Module]) --> B{Has sources?}
  B -- No --> C[/Empty state: Add first source/]
  B -- Yes --> D[/Source List with totals/]
  C --> E[Click + Add Income Source]
  D --> E
  E --> F[/Source Form Modal/]
  F --> G{Validation OK?}
  G -- No --> H[Show field errors] --> F
  G -- Yes --> I[POST /income/sources]
  I --> J[Source created in DB]
  J --> K[Invalidate dashboard cache]
  K --> D
  D --> L[Click Record Income on source]
  L --> M[/Entry Form Modal/]
  M --> N{Validation OK?}
  N -- No --> O[Show errors] --> M
  N -- Yes --> P[POST /income/entries]
  P --> Q[Write to ledger_entries debit+credit]
  Q --> R[Update monthly total]
  R --> S[Invalidate dashboard cache]
  S --> D
4.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Create Source
User creates "Infosys Salary" with type=monthly_salary, default_amount=85000, is_recurring=true
Record Income
User records June income: amount=85000, income_date=2026-06-01, no attachment
Ledger Written
Two ledger_entries created: CREDIT to income account, DEBIT offsets income pool
Dashboard Updated
Redis cache invalidated for dashboard:user:{id}:summary key
Total Shown
Monthly income card on dashboard updates to Rs.85,000. Yearly total: Rs.10,20,000
Outcome
Income tracked, ledger balanced, dashboard reflects correct totals immediately
4.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Future Date
income_date > today -> 422 "Income date cannot be in the future"
Zero Amount
amount = 0 -> 422 "Amount must be greater than zero"
Source Not Own
salary_source_id belongs to another user -> 403 Forbidden (BOLA check)
Large File
Attachment > 5MB -> 422 "File size must not exceed 5MB"
Invalid Mime
Attachment is .exe disguised as .pdf -> 422 "Only PDF, JPG, PNG files are allowed"
Duplicate Entry
Same idempotency key re-submitted -> 409 Conflict, return original response
4.5 Validation Rules
Field
Rule
Error Message
title
required|string|min:2|max:150
Income source name is required (2-150 characters)
source_type
required|exists:income_source_types,slug
Select a valid income type
is_recurring
required|boolean
Specify if this income recurs monthly
default_amount
nullable|numeric|min:1|max:99999999|decimal:0,2
Amount must be a positive number
amount
required|numeric|min:0.01|max:99999999|decimal:0,2
Enter a valid income amount
income_date
required|date|date_format:Y-m-d|before_or_equal:today
Date cannot be in the future
salary_source_id
required|exists:salary_sources,id|scope:user
Invalid income source
notes
nullable|string|max:1000
Notes must be under 1000 characters
attachment
nullable|file|mimes:pdf,jpg,jpeg,png|max:5120
Only PDF or image files up to 5MB

Trigger
Channel

First income source added
In-App
Great start! Your first income source is set up. Now record your first income entry.
Income recorded
In-App
Rs.{amount} income from {source} recorded for {month}.
No income in 35 days
Email
Reminder: No income has been recorded this month. Add your salary entry.
Yearly income milestone
In-App
Milestone! You have earned Rs.{amount} so far this financial year.
Recurring income due
Push
Your {source} income is due today. Tap to log it quickly.

4.8 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
INSERT
salary_sources
title, source_type, is_recurring, default_amount, user_id, tenant_id
INSERT
income_entries
salary_source_id, amount, income_date, month, year, financial_year, currency, exchange_rate, user_id
INSERT
ledger_entries
CREDIT entry: account_type=income, amount, posted_at, transaction_ref_type=income_entry
INSERT
ledger_entries
DEBIT entry: account_type=equity, amount (counter-entry for double-entry)
INSERT
audit_logs
action=income_entry_created, old_values=null, new_values={amount,date}
DELETE
Redis
Invalidate dashboard:user:{id}:summary cache key
SELECT
income_entries
SUM(amount) GROUP BY month,year WHERE user_id=? for summary
UPDATE
income_entries
SET deleted_at=NOW() on soft delete (preserves ledger integrity)
EXP
MODULE 5:  Expense Tracking
5.1 User Journey
The user logs individual expenses under predefined or custom categories, sets monthly budget limits per category, and receives real-time warnings when approaching or exceeding budgets. The system provides category-wise analysis and month-over-month comparison.
5.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Expenses Home
Clicks "Expenses" in sidebar
Load current month expenses, category summary cards
2
Category Filter
Selects category chip to filter
Filter expense list to selected category only
3
Add Expense
Clicks "+ Add Expense" FAB button
Open expense form modal
4
Fill Form
Fills title, amount, category, date, optional receipt
Show budget utilization preview as amount typed
5
Submit Expense
Clicks "Save Expense"
POST /expenses, show in list immediately
6
Budget Warning
Category crosses 80% of budget
Show yellow inline warning within the category card
7
Set Budget
Clicks gear icon -> "Set Budget" for a category
Open budget form, PUT /expenses/budgets
8
Expense History
Scrolls paginated list
Load more on scroll, filter by date range or category
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Expense Module]) --> B[Load current month data]
  B --> C[/Category Summary Cards + List/]
  C --> D[Click + Add Expense]
  D --> E[/Expense Form Modal/]
  E --> F{Category selected?}
  F -- Yes --> G[Show current budget utilization]
  F -- No --> E
  G --> H{Validation OK?}
  H -- No --> I[Show errors] --> E
  H -- Yes --> J[POST /expenses]
  J --> K[Write ledger_entries]
  K --> L{Budget check}
  L -- Over 100% --> M[Send budget exceeded notification]
  L -- Over 80% --> N[Send budget warning notification]
  L -- Under 80% --> O[No alert]
  M --> P[Invalidate dashboard cache]
  N --> P
  O --> P
  P --> C
5.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Add Expense
User logs "Swiggy dinner" -> category=Food, amount=450, date=2026-06-09
Budget Check
Food budget = Rs.5,000/month, spent so far = Rs.4,200 (84%) -> warning triggered
Notification
In-app notification: "You have used 84% of your Food budget this month"
Ledger Written
ledger_entries: DEBIT expense account Rs.450, CREDIT equity account Rs.450
Dashboard Updated
Redis cache invalidated, next dashboard load shows updated monthly expense total
Outcome
Expense recorded, budget alert sent, financial records balanced via double-entry
5.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
System Category Delete
User tries to delete system category (Food) -> 403 "System categories cannot be deleted"
Future Date
expense_date > today -> 422 "Expense date cannot be in the future"
Category Not Own
Custom category_id belongs to another user -> 403 Forbidden
Budget Not Set
User adds expense to category with no budget -> saved normally, no warning (budget is optional)
Receipt Too Large
Receipt image > 5MB -> 422 "File must be under 5MB"
Invalid Amount
amount = -100 -> 422 "Amount must be greater than zero"
5.5 Validation Rules
Field
Rule
Error Message
title
required|string|min:2|max:200
Expense title is required
amount
required|numeric|min:0.01|max:99999999|decimal:0,2
Enter a valid amount greater than zero
expense_category_id
required|exists:expense_categories,id
Select a valid expense category
expense_date
required|date|date_format:Y-m-d|before_or_equal:today
Date cannot be in the future
is_recurring
required|boolean
Specify if this is a recurring expense
receipt
nullable|file|mimes:pdf,jpg,jpeg,png|max:5120
Only PDF or image files up to 5MB
notes
nullable|string|max:1000
Notes must be under 1000 characters
budget_amount
required|numeric|min:1|max:99999999|decimal:0,2
Enter a valid budget amount
month
required|integer|min:1|max:12
Select a valid month
year
required|integer|min:2020|max:2100
Select a valid year
5.6 Notifications
Trigger
Channel
Message
Budget reached 80%
In-App + Push
You have used {pct}% of your {category} budget for {month}.
Budget exceeded 100%
In-App + Email
You exceeded your {category} budget by Rs.{amount} this month.
High single expense
In-App
Large expense recorded: Rs.{amount} for {title}. Is this correct?
Monthly expense milestone
In-App
Your total expenses this month are Rs.{amount}. View breakdown.
Recurring expense reminder
Push
Your recurring expense "{title}" is due today.

5.8 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
INSERT
expenses
title, amount, expense_category_id, expense_date, month, year, financial_year, is_recurring, user_id
INSERT
ledger_entries
DEBIT expense_account, CREDIT equity_account, amount, posted_at
SELECT
expense_budgets
WHERE user_id=? AND category_id=? AND month=? AND year=? for budget check
SELECT
expenses
SUM(amount) WHERE category_id=? AND month=? AND year=? for utilization
INSERT
notifications
If budget > 80%: type=budget_warning, data={category,pct,amount}
INSERT
audit_logs
action=expense_created, new_values={title,amount,category,date}
UPDATE
expenses
SET deleted_at=NOW() on soft delete
DELETE
Redis
Invalidate dashboard:user:{id}:summary cache key
INSERT
expense_budgets
category_id, budget_amount, month, year, user_id on budget set
SAV
MODULE 6:  Savings Management
6.1 User Journey
The user creates named savings buckets for specific purposes (Vacation, House Down Payment, Vehicle), sets a target amount and optional deadline, then records deposits and withdrawals. The system tracks progress, calculates completion percentages, and projects completion dates.
6.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Savings Home
Clicks "Savings" in sidebar
Load all saving_accounts with progress bars
2
Create Bucket
Clicks "+ New Savings Goal"
Open bucket form: name, type, target, date
3
Bucket Created
Submits form
POST /savings/accounts, show new bucket with 0% progress
4
Add Deposit
Clicks "Deposit" on a bucket
Open deposit modal: amount, date, notes
5
Deposit Saved
Submits deposit
POST /savings/{id}/deposit, update progress bar
6
Withdraw Funds
Clicks "Withdraw" (with warning prompt)
POST /savings/{id}/withdraw, update balance
7
Transaction History
Clicks bucket name to expand
Load saving_transactions list for that bucket
8
Bucket Complete
current_amount reaches target_amount
Show celebration, mark complete, send notification
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Savings Module]) --> B[Load saving accounts]
  B --> C[/Savings buckets with progress bars/]
  C --> D[Click + New Savings Goal]
  D --> E[/Bucket Form/]
  E --> F{Validation OK?}
  F -- No --> G[Show errors] --> E
  F -- Yes --> H[POST /savings/accounts]
  H --> C
  C --> I[Click Deposit on bucket]
  I --> J[/Deposit Modal/]
  J --> K{Amount valid?}
  K -- No --> L[Show error] --> J
  K -- Yes --> M[POST /savings/deposit]
  M --> N[UPDATE current_amount]
  N --> O[INSERT ledger_entries]
  O --> P{Reached target?}
  P -- Yes --> Q[Send completion notification]
  P -- No --> R{Over 75%?}
  R -- Yes --> S[Send milestone notification]
  R --> C
  Q --> C
  C --> T[Click Withdraw]
  T --> U{amount <= current_amount?}
  U -- No --> V[Error: insufficient balance] --> C
  U -- Yes --> W[POST /savings/withdraw]
  W --> C
6.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Create Bucket
User creates "Goa Vacation" bucket: target=Rs.50,000, target_date=2026-12-31
First Deposit
User deposits Rs.10,000 -> current_amount=10,000, completion=20%
Progress Shown
Progress bar fills to 20%. "Rs.40,000 remaining. On track for Dec 2026"
Monthly Save
User deposits Rs.8,000 each month. At month 5: Rs.50,000 reached
Completion
Celebration animation shown. Notification: "Congratulations! Goa Vacation goal achieved!"
Outcome
Goal completed, ledger balanced, history preserved for all deposit transactions
6.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Withdraw Excess
Withdraw Rs.15,000 from bucket with Rs.10,000 -> 422 "Withdrawal cannot exceed current balance of Rs.10,000"
Past Target Date
target_date in the past -> 422 "Target date must be a future date"
Zero Deposit
Deposit amount = 0 -> 422 "Deposit amount must be greater than zero"
Bucket Not Own
saving_account_id belongs to another user -> 403 Forbidden
Delete Active
User tries to delete bucket with balance > 0 -> 422 "Please withdraw all funds before deleting this bucket"
6.5 Validation Rules
Field
Rule
Error Message
name
required|string|min:2|max:150
Savings bucket name is required
bucket_type
required|exists:saving_bucket_types,slug
Select a valid savings type
target_amount
required|numeric|min:1|max:999999999|decimal:0,2
Enter a valid target amount
target_date
nullable|date|after:today
Target date must be in the future
amount (deposit)
required|numeric|min:0.01|max:99999999|decimal:0,2
Enter a valid deposit amount
amount (withdraw)
required|numeric|min:0.01|max:current_amount
Withdrawal cannot exceed current balance
transaction_date
required|date|date_format:Y-m-d|before_or_equal:today
Date cannot be in the future
notes
nullable|string|max:1000
Notes must be under 1000 characters

Behind schedule

6.8 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
INSERT
saving_accounts
name, bucket_type, target_amount, current_amount=0, target_date, user_id
INSERT
saving_transactions
saving_account_id, transaction_type=deposit, amount, transaction_date, user_id
UPDATE
saving_accounts
SET current_amount = current_amount + deposit_amount WHERE id=?
INSERT
ledger_entries
CREDIT savings_account, DEBIT equity on deposit
INSERT
goal_milestones
Auto-create milestones at 25%, 50%, 75%, 100% on bucket creation
UPDATE
goal_milestones
SET achieved_at=NOW() when threshold crossed
INSERT
notifications
type=savings_milestone, data={bucket_name,percentage} when milestone hit
INSERT
audit_logs
action=saving_deposit, old_values={prev_balance}, new_values={new_balance}
EMF
MODULE 7:  Emergency Fund
7.1 User Journey
The user sets up their emergency fund by entering average monthly expenses. The system calculates the recommended 6-month target (customizable to 3-12 months), tracks the current fund balance, shows the gap, and provides a monthly deposit plan to reach the target within a chosen timeline.
7.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Emergency Fund Home
Clicks "Emergency Fund" in sidebar
Check if emergency_fund record exists for user
2
Setup Screen
First visit: shown setup wizard if no record
Prompt: enter average monthly expenses
3
Setup Complete
User enters monthly_expenses, selects months(6)
POST /emergency-fund, calculate required_amount
4
Fund Dashboard
Sees: required, current, gap, and progress bar
Load from emergency_funds table
5
Add Funds
Clicks "Add to Fund" button
Open deposit modal: amount, date
6
Deposit Saved
Submits deposit
POST /emergency-fund/deposit, update current_amount
7
Gap Analysis
Clicks "View Gap Analysis" link
Show: monthly target to close gap in X months
8
Update Expenses
Clicks "Update Monthly Expenses"
Recalculate required_amount with new base
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Emergency Fund Module]) --> B{Fund exists?}
  B -- No --> C[/Setup Wizard/]
  C --> D[Enter monthly_expenses]
  D --> E[Select target months 3-12]
  E --> F[POST /emergency-fund]
  F --> G[Calculate required = expenses x months]
  G --> H[/Fund Dashboard/]
  B -- Yes --> H
  H --> I[Show: Required vs Current vs Gap]
  I --> J[Click Add to Fund]
  J --> K[/Deposit Modal/]
  K --> L{Amount valid?}
  L -- No --> M[Error] --> K
  L -- Yes --> N[POST /emergency-fund/deposit]
  N --> O[UPDATE current_amount]
  O --> P{Gap closed?}
  P -- Yes --> Q[Send completion notification]
  P -- No --> R{Over 50%?}
  R -- Yes --> S[Send milestone notification]
  P --> H
  Q --> H
  S --> H
7.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Setup
User enters monthly expenses = Rs.30,000, selects 6 months target
Calculation
required_amount = 30,000 x 6 = Rs.1,80,000. Gap = Rs.1,80,000 (0% funded)
First Deposit
User deposits Rs.20,000. current_amount=20,000, coverage=0.67 months (11%)
Monthly Plan
Gap analysis shows: deposit Rs.16,000/month to reach target in 10 months
Milestone
At Rs.90,000 (50%): "Your emergency fund now covers 3 months of expenses!"
Completion
At Rs.1,80,000: "Emergency fund fully funded! You have 6 months of security."
Outcome
User has clear visibility of emergency preparedness with guided monthly deposit plan
7.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Zero Expenses
monthly_expenses = 0 -> 422 "Monthly expenses must be greater than zero"
Invalid Months
recommended_months outside 1-24 -> 422 "Target months must be between 1 and 24"
Excess Deposit
Deposit would exceed required_amount by more than 20% -> warning shown, proceed allowed
Duplicate Setup
User tries POST when fund already exists -> 409 "Emergency fund already configured. Use update endpoint"
Update Fail
New monthly_expenses reduces required, current_amount now exceeds required -> advisory shown, no error

GOL
MODULE 8:  Financial Goals
8.1 User Journey
The user creates financial goals (Buy House, Buy Car, Child Education, Retirement) with a target amount and deadline. The system calculates inflation-adjusted targets, required monthly savings, and provides three scenario projections. Users log contributions, track milestones, and receive guidance when falling behind.
8.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Goals Home
Clicks "Goals" in sidebar
Load all active goals sorted by priority
2
Create Goal
Clicks "+ New Goal"
Open goal form: name, type, target, date, priority
3
Projection Preview
After entering target and date
Auto-calculate monthly savings needed inline
4
Goal Created
Submits form
POST /goals, show new goal with projection
5
Goal Detail
Clicks on a goal card
Full detail: timeline, contributions history, milestones
6
Add Contribution
Clicks "Add Contribution" button
Open contribution modal: amount, date, notes
7
View Projection
Clicks "View Full Projection"
Show month-by-month timeline with 3 scenarios
8
Edit Goal
Clicks edit icon
Update target, date, inflation rate
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Goals Module]) --> B[Load all goals]
  B --> C[/Goals list with priority order/]
  C --> D[Click + New Goal]
  D --> E[/Goal Form/]
  E --> F[Enter target_amount + target_date]
  F --> G[Auto-calc: monthly_required shown inline]
  G --> H{Validation OK?}
  H -- No --> I[Show errors] --> E
  H -- Yes --> J[POST /goals]
  J --> K[Run GoalProjectionService]
  K --> L[Store goal_projections record]
  L --> C
  C --> M[Click goal card]
  M --> N[/Goal Detail Page/]
  N --> O[Click Add Contribution]
  O --> P[/Contribution Modal/]
  P --> Q{amount <= remaining?}
  Q -- No --> R[Warning: exceeds target] --> P
  Q -- Yes --> S[POST /goals/contribution]
  S --> T[UPDATE current_amount]
  T --> U{Milestone crossed?}
  U -- Yes --> V[Send milestone notification]
  U --> N
  V --> N
8.3 Financial Projection Calculations
Inflation-Adjusted Target
target x (1 + inflation_rate/100) ^ years_remaining
Monthly Saving Required
(adjusted_target - current_amount) / months_remaining
Progress %
(current_amount / adjusted_target) x 100
Expected Completion Date
current_date + ceil((adjusted_target - current) / monthly_avg_contribution) months
Optimistic Scenario
Assumes 2% lower inflation + 3% extra return on saved funds
Pessimistic Scenario
Assumes 2% higher inflation + 0% return on saved funds
On-Track Flag
TRUE if actual monthly average >= monthly_required
8.4 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Create Goal
User creates "Buy House in Pune": target=Rs.50L, date=2032-01-01, inflation=6%
Projection
Adjusted target=Rs.70.9L (6 years at 6% inflation). Monthly required=Rs.60,420
First Contribution
User adds Rs.50,000 contribution. current_amount=50,000, progress=0.7%
Milestone
At 25% (Rs.17.7L): "You are 25% towards your House goal! Keep going!"
On Track Check
System checks if monthly avg contributions >= Rs.60,420. Shows status badge
Outcome
User has realistic, inflation-adjusted goal with clear monthly saving target
8.5 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Past Target Date
target_date <= today -> 422 "Target date must be in the future"
Excess Contribution
contribution > remaining_amount -> warning shown (not error), user may confirm
Goal Conflict
Total monthly_required for all goals > monthly savings capacity -> advisory alert shown
Paused Goal Contribute
Adding contribution to paused goal -> 422 "Resume goal before adding contributions"
Zero Target
target_amount = 0 -> 422 "Target amount must be greater than zero"

INV
MODULE 9:  Investment Tracking
9.1 User Journey
The user adds investment portfolios across multiple instrument types (Mutual Funds, Stocks, PPF, FD, NPS, Gold, Crypto). They record buy/sell/SIP transactions, update current values, and view XIRR, CAGR, and portfolio allocation. The system calculates profit/loss and compares against benchmarks.
9.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Investments Home
Clicks "Investments" in sidebar
Load portfolio summary: total invested, current value, P&L, XIRR
2
Allocation Chart
Views donut chart by asset class
Show equity/debt/gold/crypto/cash % breakdown
3
Add Investment
Clicks "+ Add Investment"
Open form: type, name, symbol, invested, purchase_date
4
Investment Created
Submits form
POST /investments, show in portfolio list
5
Log Transaction
Clicks "+" on an investment
Open transaction form: type(buy/sell/sip/dividend), amount, units, date
6
Update Value
Clicks "Update Value" on investment
Enter current_value -> PUT /investments/{id}
7
View Detail
Clicks investment name
Show: all transactions, XIRR, CAGR, vs benchmark chart
8
SIP Schedule
Clicks "Set up SIP"
Configure recurring SIP: amount, frequency, next_due_date
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Investments Module]) --> B[Load portfolio]
  B --> C[/Portfolio Summary + List/]
  C --> D[Click + Add Investment]
  D --> E[/Investment Form/]
  E --> F{Validation OK?}
  F -- No --> G[Show errors] --> E
  F -- Yes --> H[POST /investments]
  H --> I[Calculate initial P&L]
  I --> J[Queue XIRR computation job]
  J --> C
  C --> K[Click investment card]
  K --> L[/Investment Detail/]
  L --> M[View XIRR + CAGR]
  L --> N[Click Add Transaction]
  N --> O[/Transaction Form/]
  O --> P{Type?}
  P -- buy/sip --> Q[UPDATE invested_amount + units]
  P -- sell --> R[Calculate realized gain STCG/LTCG]
  P -- dividend --> S[Record income, no unit change]
  Q --> T[Recompute XIRR nightly job]
  R --> T
  S --> T
  T --> C
9.3 Investment Calculation Definitions
Absolute Return %
(current_value - invested_amount) / invested_amount x 100
XIRR
Extended IRR via Newton-Raphson: accounts for each SIP installment date and amount
CAGR
For investments > 1 year: (current_value/invested_amount)^(1/years) - 1 x 100
Profit / Loss
current_value - invested_amount (negative = loss)
STCG
Gain on equity/MF held < 1 year: taxed at 20%
LTCG
Gain on equity/MF held > 1 year above Rs.1.25L: taxed at 12.5%
Portfolio Alloc %
asset_class current_value / total_portfolio_value x 100 per class
Units
Tracked per transaction: total_units = SUM(buy_units) - SUM(sell_units)
9.4 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Add Investment
User adds Axis Bluechip MF: type=Mutual Fund, invested=Rs.1,00,000, date=2024-01-01
SIP Set Up
User sets SIP: Rs.5,000/month, frequency=monthly, start=2024-02-01
Monthly SIP
Each month: transaction_type=sip logged with amount=5,000 and NAV-based units
Update Value
User updates current_value=Rs.1,75,000 (after 18 months, Rs.90,000 invested via SIP)
XIRR Computed
Nightly job: XIRR=22.4% p.a. (vs simple ROI which would show 75% absolute - misleading)
View Returns
Dashboard shows: Invested=Rs.1,90,000, Current=Rs.1,75,000 (correction), XIRR=22.4%, CAGR=N/A (not 1yr old yet)
Outcome
User sees accurate XIRR returns including SIP timing effect, can compare vs Nifty 50 benchmark
9.5 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Sell More Than Owned
sell_units > current_units -> 422 "Cannot sell more units than you own"
Future Purchase Date
purchase_date > today -> 422 "Purchase date cannot be in the future"
Maturity Before Start
maturity_date <= purchase_date -> 422 "Maturity date must be after purchase date"
Invalid Symbol
symbol with special chars -> 422 "Symbol must contain only letters and numbers"
Negative Value
current_value < 0 -> 422 "Current value cannot be negative"
Investment Not Own
investment_id belongs to another user -> 403 Forbidden

MODULE 10:  Debt Management
10.1 User Journey
The user adds active loans and debts (home loan, car loan, credit card, personal loan), records EMI payments, views the full amortization schedule, tracks outstanding balance reduction, and optionally compares debt payoff strategies (Avalanche vs Snowball) for optimal repayment.
10.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Debt Home
Clicks "Debts" in sidebar
Load all active debts with outstanding amounts
2
Add Debt
Clicks "+ Add Loan/Debt"
Open form: type, lender, principal, rate, EMI, start_date
3
Schedule Generated
Debt created
POST /debts, generate full amortization schedule in background
4
Debt Dashboard
Clicks on a debt card
Show: schedule, paid/remaining EMIs, interest paid, foreclosure amount
5
Record Payment
Clicks "Record EMI Payment"
Open payment form: amount, date, principal/interest split, mode
6
Payment Saved
Submits payment
POST /debts/{id}/payments, update schedule, recalculate outstanding
7
Prepayment
Clicks "Make Prepayment"
Enter prepayment amount, system recalculates remaining schedule
8
Strategy View
Clicks "Payoff Strategy"
Show Avalanche vs Snowball comparison with extra monthly amount slider
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Debt Module]) --> B[Load all debts]
  B --> C[/Debt list with totals/]
  C --> D[Click + Add Debt]
  D --> E[/Debt Form/]
  E --> F{Validation OK?}
  F -- No --> G[Show errors] --> E
  F -- Yes --> H[POST /debts]
  H --> I[Generate amortization schedule job]
  I --> J[INSERT debt_amortization_schedule rows]
  J --> C
  C --> K[Click debt card]
  K --> L[/Debt Detail with Schedule/]
  L --> M[Click Record Payment]
  M --> N[/Payment Form/]
  N --> O{Payment valid?}
  O -- No --> P[Error] --> N
  O -- Yes --> Q[POST /debts/payments]
  Q --> R[UPDATE amortization_schedule row status=paid]
  R --> S[UPDATE debts.outstanding_amount]
  S --> T[UPDATE debts.paid_emis + 1]
  T --> U{All EMIs paid?}
  U -- Yes --> V[SET debts.status=closed]
  U -- No --> L
  V --> W[Send debt closed celebration] --> C
10.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Add Debt
User adds HDFC Home Loan: principal=Rs.50L, rate=8.5%, EMI=Rs.43,391, tenure=180 months
Schedule
180-row amortization schedule generated with monthly principal/interest breakdown
Record EMI
User records June EMI: Rs.43,391 (principal=Rs.7,891, interest=Rs.35,500)
Schedule Updated
Row 1 in debt_amortization_schedule marked as paid. Outstanding=Rs.49,92,109
Outstanding
Debt card shows: Outstanding Rs.49,92,109, Interest paid Rs.35,500, EMIs: 1/180
Prepayment
User makes Rs.2,00,000 prepayment. System regenerates schedule: now 168 months remaining
Outcome
User has full transparency on debt progress, interest costs, and prepayment impact
10.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Outstanding > Principal
outstanding_amount > principal_amount -> 422 "Outstanding cannot exceed principal amount"
Payment > Outstanding
payment_amount > outstanding_amount -> warning shown (possible full closure), user confirms
End Before Start
end_date <= start_date -> 422 "End date must be after start date"
Closed Debt Payment
Recording payment on closed debt -> 422 "This debt is already closed"
Negative Rate
interest_rate < 0 -> 422 "Interest rate cannot be negative"
Invalid EMI Count
total_emis > 600 -> 422 "Maximum loan tenure is 50 years (600 months)"

10.8 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
INSERT
debts
debt_type, name, principal_amount, outstanding_amount, interest_rate, emi_amount, start_date, user_id
INSERT
debt_amortization_schedule
180 rows for home loan: emi_number, due_date, emi_amount, principal, interest, opening/closing balance
INSERT
debt_payments
debt_id, payment_amount, principal_component, interest_component, payment_date, payment_mode
UPDATE
debts
SET outstanding_amount -= principal_component, paid_emis += 1
UPDATE
debt_amortization_schedule
SET status=paid, paid_date=NOW() for the corresponding emi_number
DELETE
debt_amortization_schedule
DELETE remaining rows on prepayment, then re-INSERT recalculated schedule
UPDATE
debts
SET status=closed, updated_at=NOW() when paid_emis=total_emis
INSERT
ledger_entries
DEBIT debt_account (reduces liability), CREDIT equity on payment
RPT
MODULE 11:  Reports & Analytics
11.1 User Journey
The user accesses the reports module to view detailed financial analysis across monthly, quarterly, and yearly periods. They can compare periods, view income vs expense trends, check savings growth, monitor investment performance, track goal progress, and export reports as PDF, Excel, or CSV. All heavy reports are generated asynchronously.
11.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Reports Home
Clicks "Reports" in sidebar
Load report menu: Monthly, Quarterly, Yearly, Health Score
2
Period Selector
Selects month/year or quarter
Show date range selector with quick picks
3
Monthly Report
Selects Monthly Report
POST /reports/jobs (async), show "Generating..." state
4
Job Polling
Client polls GET /reports/jobs/{id}
Poll every 3s, max 30s before timeout message
5
Report Ready
Job completes, report displayed
Show full report with charts: income/expense, categories, trends
6
Compare Mode
Toggles "Compare with previous period"
Load both periods side-by-side with delta columns
7
Export
Clicks "Export PDF" or "Export Excel"
GET /reports/export/pdf?month=6&year=2026 -> file download
8
Health Score
Clicks "Financial Health Score"
GET /reports/health-score, show score breakdown
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Reports Module]) --> B[/Report Type Selector/]
  B --> C{Type?}
  C -- Monthly --> D[POST /reports/jobs type=monthly]
  C -- Quarterly --> E[POST /reports/jobs type=quarterly]
  C -- Yearly --> F[POST /reports/jobs type=yearly]
  C -- Health Score --> G[GET /reports/health-score cached]
  D --> H[Queue report generation job]
  E --> H
  F --> H
  H --> I[Return job_id immediately 202]
  I --> J[Client polls GET /jobs/id every 3s]
  J --> K{Job done?}
  K -- No --> L{Timeout 30s?}
  L -- No --> J
  L -- Yes --> M[Show retry button]
  K -- Yes --> N[/Report displayed with charts/]
  N --> O{Export?}
  O -- PDF --> P[GET /export/pdf -> download]
  O -- Excel --> Q[GET /export/excel -> download]
  O -- CSV --> R[GET /export/csv -> download]
  G --> S[/Health Score breakdown/]
11.3 Financial Health Score Breakdown
Savings Rate Score (30%)
30% if savings_rate>=30%. Linear scale. 0% if savings_rate<=0%
Emergency Fund Score (25%)
25% if fund covers 6+ months. Proportional below 6 months
Debt-to-Income Score (25%)
25% if total_EMIs/monthly_income <= 30%. Decreasing above 30%
Investment Score (20%)
20% if investment_value >= 3x monthly_income. Proportional below
Total Health Score
Sum of four component scores (0-100). Updated monthly
Score Bands
0-40: Critical | 41-60: Needs Attention | 61-80: Good | 81-100: Excellent
11.4 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Generate Report
User requests Monthly Report for June 2026. Job queued, job_id returned
Job Completes
Background job aggregates income, expense, savings, investment data. Takes 2-4 seconds
Charts Loaded
Income vs Expense bar chart, Category pie chart, Savings trend line shown
Compare Mode
Toggle "vs May 2026": side-by-side table shows +15% income, -8% expenses
Export PDF
User clicks Export PDF: DomPDF generates 4-page report, download link returned
Health Score
Health Score = 72/100. Savings(26/30), Emergency(20/25), Debt(17/25), Investment(9/20)
Outcome
User has complete financial analysis with exportable report and actionable insights
11.5 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
No Data for Period
No income/expense records for selected month -> report shows zeros with "No data recorded for this period"
Job Timeout
Report generation > 30s (large data set) -> "Report taking longer than expected. We will email it when ready"
Export Fails
DomPDF memory error on large dataset -> 500, "Export failed. Try selecting a shorter date range"
Concurrent Reports
User submits 5 report jobs simultaneously -> 429 "Maximum 2 concurrent report jobs"
Future Period
Request report for future month -> 422 "Cannot generate report for future periods"
11.6 Notifications
Trigger
Channel
Message
Monthly report ready
Email
Your June 2026 Financial Report is ready. Key insight: Savings rate improved by 5%.
Report emailed (long job)
Email
Your report took longer than expected. Download it here: {link}
Health score improved
In-App
Your financial health score improved from {old} to {new}/100 this month!
Health score declined
In-App
Your financial health score dropped to {score}/100. View what changed.
Yearly summary
Email
Your Annual Financial Summary for FY{year} is ready. Net worth grew by {pct}%.

11.8 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
SELECT
income_entries
SUM(amount) GROUP BY month,year,salary_source_id WHERE user_id=?
SELECT
expenses
SUM(amount) GROUP BY expense_category_id,month,year WHERE user_id=?
SELECT
financial_snapshots
WHERE user_id=? ORDER BY snapshot_date for net worth history
SELECT
expense_budgets
JOIN expenses for budget variance calculation per category
SELECT
expense_trends
WHERE user_id=? for anomaly detection display
INSERT
financial_health_scores
Computed scores stored for trend history tracking
INSERT
audit_logs
action=report_generated, type=monthly, action=report_exported
SET
Redis
reports:user:{id}:monthly:{y}:{m} = JSON, EX 3600 (1hr TTL)
NOT
MODULE 12:  Notification Center
12.1 User Journey
The user receives real-time financial alerts, milestone celebrations, reminders, and system messages through multiple channels: in-app notification center, email, and push notifications (mobile). They can mark notifications as read, configure preferences per category, and view full notification history.
12.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Bell Icon
Clicks notification bell in header
Show dropdown with last 5 unread notifications + count badge
2
View All
Clicks "View All Notifications"
Navigate to /notifications full list, paginated
3
Mark Read
Clicks a notification
POST /notifications/{id}/read, navigate to relevant module
4
Mark All Read
Clicks "Mark All as Read"
POST /notifications/read-all, badge clears
5
Preferences
Clicks "Notification Settings" gear
Show toggle matrix: type x channel (in-app/email/push)
6
Save Preferences
Toggles and saves preferences
PUT /notifications/preferences, apply to future notifications
7
Delete
Swipe left on notification
DELETE /notifications/{id}, remove from list
8
Push Registration
On mobile app install
POST /me/device-tokens, register FCM/APNs token
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A[Financial Event occurs] --> B{Notification triggered?}
  B -- Yes --> C[Create Notification record in DB]
  C --> D[Load user preferences]
  D --> E{In-App enabled?}
  E -- Yes --> F[Insert into notifications table]
  F --> G[Increment unread badge count in Redis]
  D --> H{Email enabled?}
  H -- Yes --> I[Queue email notification job]
  I --> J[Send via SMTP/Mailgun]
  D --> K{Push enabled and device token exists?}
  K -- Yes --> L[Queue push notification job]
  L --> M[Send via FCM or APNs]
  B -- No --> N[Skip - preference disabled]
  F --> O[/User sees badge on bell/]
  O --> P[User clicks notification]
  P --> Q[POST /notifications/id/read]
  Q --> R[SET read_at=NOW()]
  R --> S[Redirect to relevant module]
12.3 Notification Type Registry
budget_warning
Category budget reached 80% of monthly limit
budget_exceeded
Category budget exceeded 100%
goal_milestone
Financial goal reached 25/50/75/100% milestone
goal_behind_schedule
Goal contributions falling behind required monthly amount
savings_milestone
Savings bucket reached a progress milestone
emergency_fund_alert
Emergency fund below recommended threshold
emi_reminder
Loan EMI due in 3 days
debt_closed
All EMIs paid, loan fully repaid
investment_update
XIRR/CAGR recalculated, significant portfolio movement
sip_due
SIP installment due today for a tracked investment
login_new_device
Successful login from an unrecognized device
report_ready
Async report generation completed, ready to view
income_reminder
No income entry recorded after 35 days of month
tax_reminder
Financial year-end approaching (Feb/Mar alert)

12.6 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
INSERT
notifications
id(UUID), type, notifiable_type=User, notifiable_id, data JSON, read_at=NULL
UPDATE
notifications
SET read_at=NOW() WHERE id=? AND notifiable_id=current_user
UPDATE
notifications
SET read_at=NOW() WHERE notifiable_id=? AND read_at IS NULL (read-all)
DELETE
notifications
WHERE id=? AND notifiable_id=? on user delete

notifications
WHERE notifiable_id=? AND read_at IS NULL for unread count

Redis
notifications:unread:{user_id} counter for badge count
INSERT
device_tokens
user_id, platform, token, last_used=NOW(), is_active=1
UPDATE
device_tokens
SET last_used=NOW() on each successful push delivery
PRF
MODULE 13:  Profile & Settings
13.1 User Journey
The user manages their account profile, security settings (password, 2FA, trusted devices), notification preferences, data privacy controls (DPDP), subscription plan, and account deletion. Settings are grouped by category with clear, reversible actions and confirmation prompts for destructive operations.
13.2 Screen Flow
#
Screen
User Action
System Response
1
Profile Page
Clicks avatar or "Settings" in sidebar
Load profile data, subscription status, last login
2
Edit Profile
Clicks "Edit Profile"
Inline editing: name, phone, avatar upload
3
Save Profile
Clicks "Save Changes"
PUT /me, validate and update users table
4
Change Password
Clicks "Security" tab -> "Change Password"
Require current password, enter new, confirm
5
Enable 2FA
Clicks "Enable Two-Factor Auth"
Show QR code for authenticator app, verify code to confirm
6
Privacy Tab
Clicks "Privacy & Data" tab
Show: consent status, data requests, export option
7
Data Export
Clicks "Download My Data"
Queue export job, email download link when ready
8
Delete Account
Clicks "Delete Account"
Show 3-step confirmation: type "DELETE", password, final confirm
9
Plan Tab
Clicks "Subscription" tab
Show current plan, usage stats, upgrade options
Flow Diagram (Mermaid):
flowchart TD
  A([Profile Settings]) --> B[/Settings Tabs/]
  B --> C[Profile Tab]
  B --> D[Security Tab]
  B --> E[Privacy Tab]
  B --> F[Notifications Tab]
  B --> G[Subscription Tab]
  C --> H[Edit name/phone/avatar]
  H --> I[PUT /me] --> J[Update users table]
  D --> K[Change Password]
  K --> L{Current password valid?}
  L -- No --> M[Error] --> K
  L -- Yes --> N[UPDATE password hash]
  N --> O[Invalidate all other tokens]
  N --> P[Send password changed email]
  D --> Q[Enable 2FA]
  Q --> R[Generate TOTP secret]
  R --> S[Show QR code]
  S --> T[User scans + enters code]
  T --> U{Code valid?}
  U -- No --> V[Error, show again] --> S
  U -- Yes --> W[SET two_factor_secret, send confirm email]
  E --> X[Request data export]
  X --> Y[Queue export job]
  Y --> Z[Email download link]
  E --> AA[Request account deletion]
  AA --> AB{3-step confirm done?}
  AB -- No --> AC[Block deletion]
  AB -- Yes --> AD[Schedule deletion 30 days]
13.3 Success Scenario
SUCCESS FLOW
Update Profile
User updates phone: 9876543210. Validated, users table updated, audit log written
Change Password
Current password verified, new password set, all tokens except current invalidated
Enable 2FA
QR code scanned with Google Authenticator, code verified, two_factor_secret saved
Data Export
User requests export. Job queued. Email arrives in 10 minutes with download link (expires 24h)
Upload Avatar
User uploads 200KB JPEG. Stored in S3 with UUID key. Signed URL returned for display
Outcome
User has full control over profile, security, privacy, and data portability
13.4 Failure Scenarios
FAILURE FLOWS
Wrong Current Password
Password change attempted with wrong current password -> 422 "Current password is incorrect"
Invalid 2FA Code
Incorrect TOTP during 2FA enable -> 422 "Invalid verification code. Check your authenticator app"
Avatar Too Large
Avatar > 2MB -> 422 "Profile picture must be under 2MB"
Incomplete Delete Confirm
Typed "delete" instead of "DELETE" -> 422 "Please type DELETE in capitals to confirm"
Data Export Pending
User requests second export while first is still processing -> 429 "Export already in progress"
Email Change
Changing email to one already in use -> 422 "This email is already registered"
13.5 Validation Rules
Field
Rule
Error Message
name
required|string|min:2|max:100
Name must be 2-100 characters
phone
nullable|regex:/^[6-9][0-9]{9}$/
Enter a valid 10-digit Indian mobile number
avatar
nullable|file|mimes:jpg,jpeg,png|max:2048
Profile picture must be JPG/PNG under 2MB
current_password
required|string|current_password
Current password is incorrect
password
required|string|min:8|max:128|confirmed
New password must be at least 8 characters
two_factor_code
required|string|size:6|numeric
Enter the 6-digit code from your authenticator app
currency
nullable|string|size:3|in:INR,USD,EUR,GBP,AED
Select a valid currency
timezone
nullable|timezone|max:50
Select a valid timezone
delete_confirmation
required|string|in:DELETE
Please type DELETE in capitals to confirm

13.8 Database Operations
Operation
Table
Action / Query
UPDATE
users
SET name, phone, currency, timezone, updated_at=NOW()
UPDATE
users
SET avatar=s3_key after file_upload scan confirmed clean
UPDATE
users
SET password=bcrypt(new) on password change
DELETE
personal_access_tokens
WHERE tokenable_id=user_id AND id != current_token_id on pw change
UPDATE
users
SET two_factor_secret=encrypted_secret, two_factor_recovery_codes on enable
UPDATE
users
SET two_factor_secret=NULL on disable
INSERT
consent_records
user_id, consent_type, version, consented_at or withdrawn_at
INSERT
data_deletion_requests
user_id, request_type=account_closure, scheduled_deletion_at=NOW()+30days
INSERT
audit_logs
Every profile change logged: action, old_values, new_values, ip_address
